function Mmenu(mid,mtype){
document.getElementById("tmenu0"+mid).src="/images2/topmenu_"+mtype+"_0"+mid+".jpg";
	for(i=1;i<7;i++){
		if(i==mid){
	document.getElementById("smenu0"+mid).style.display="block";
		}else{
	document.getElementById("smenu0"+i).style.display="none";
		}
	}
}

function fpoll_submit(f)
{
    var chk = false;
    for (i=0; i<f.gb_poll.length;i ++) {
        if (f.gb_poll[i].checked == true) {
            chk = f.gb_poll[i].value;
            break;
        }
    }

    
    if (!chk) {
        alert("í•­ëª©ì„ ì„ íƒí•˜ì„¸ìš”");
        return false;
    }

    win_poll();
    return true;
}

{

}

<script type="text/javascript">
function tap(v,tb){
	for(var i = 0; i < 2 ; i++)
	{
		if(i == v)
		{
			document.getElementById(tb+'_'+ v).className="on_tabs"
			document.getElementById(tb+'_v_'+ v).style.display="block";
		}
	  else
	  {
			document.getElementById(tb+'_'+ i).className="off_tabs"
			document.getElementById(tb+'_v_'+ i).style.display="none";
	  }
	}
}
 
function tap3(v,tb){
	for(var i = 0; i < 3 ; i++)
	{
		if(i == v)
		{
			document.getElementById(tb+'_'+ v).className="on_tabs3"
			document.getElementById(tb+'_v_'+ v).style.display="block";
		}
	  else
	  {
			document.getElementById(tb+'_'+ i).className="off_tabs3"
			document.getElementById(tb+'_v_'+ i).style.display="none";
	  }
	}
}
</script>
